[Failure 1] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Among the cities belonging to the country named Arroyo, calculate the percentage of increase in the population in these cities from 2010 to 2020.
BIRD Evidence: DIVIDE(SUBTRACT(SUM(population_2020)), SUM(population_2010)), SUM(population_2010) as percentage where county = 'ARROYO';
Gold DB: address | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: geo | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (SUM(c2020.population) - SUM(c2010.population)) * 100.0 / SUM(c2010.population) AS percentage_increase
FROM city c2020
JOIN city c2010 ON c2020.city_name = c2010.city_name AND c2020.state_name = c2010.state_name
WHERE c2020.country_name LIKE '%Arroyo%' AND c2010.country_name LIKE '%Arroyo%'
  AND c2020.population IS NOT NULL AND c2010.population IS NOT NULL
  AND c2020.population > c2010.population;

Selected DB: scholar | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT

[Failure 18] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Among all publications containing keywords 'Turbulent Fluids', what percentage of them was published in the journal named 'Physics of Fluids'?
BIRD Evidence: 'Physics of Fluids' is the FullName of journal; percentage = DIVIDE(SUM(Keyword = 'Turbulent Fluids'), SUM(FullName = 'Physics of Fluids')) as percentage
Gold DB: authors | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: academic | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (COUNT(CASE WHEN j.name = 'Physics of Fluids' THEN 1 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*)) 
FROM 
    publication p
JOIN 
    publication_keyword pk ON p.pid = pk.pid
JOIN 
    keyword k ON pk.kid = k.kid
LEFT JOIN 
    journal j ON p.jid = j.jid
WHERE 
    k.keyword = 'Turbulent Fluids';

[Failure 42] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What is the ratio of customer to subscriber that making a trip inside Mountain View city?
BIRD Evidence: customer refers to subscription_type = 'customer'; subscriber refers to subscription_type = 'subscriber'; ratio = MULTIPLY(DIVIDE(COUNT(subscription_type = 'Customer'), COUNT(subscription_type = 'Subscriber'). 1.0)) AS ratio;
Gold DB: bike_share_1 | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: driving_school | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    COUNT(DISTINCT c.customer_id) * 1.0 / COUNT(DISTINCT s.staff_id) 
FROM 
    Customers c
JOIN 
    Addresses ca ON c.customer_address_id = ca.address_id
CROSS JOIN 
    Staff s
JOIN 
    Addresses sa ON s.staff_address_id = sa.address_id
WHERE 
    ca.city LIKE 'Mountain View' 
    AND sa.city LIKE 'Mountain View';

[Failure 53] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: For the quantities, what percent more did the store in Fremont sell than the store in Portland in 1993?
BIRD Evidence: qty is abbreviation for quantity; Fremont and Portland are name of city; sell in 1993 refers to YEAR(ord_date) = 1993; percentage = DIVIDE(
SUBTRACT(SUM(qty where city = ‘Fremont’ and year(ord_date = 1993)), 
SUM(qty where city = ‘Portland’ and year(ord_date = 1993))), SUM(qty where city = ‘Fremont’ and year(ord_date = 1993)) *100
Gold DB: book_publishing_company | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: retail_world | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (SUM(CASE WHEN c.City = 'Fremont' THEN od.Quantity ELSE 0 END) - 
     SUM(CASE WHEN c.City = 'Portland' THEN od.Quantity ELSE 0 END)) * 100.0 / 
    NULLIF(SUM(CASE WHEN c.City = 'Portland' THEN od.Quantity ELSE 0 END), 0) AS PercentMore
FROM OrderDetails od
JOIN Orders o ON od.OrderID = o.OrderID
JOIN Customers c ON o.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
WHERE strftime('%Y', o.OrderDate) = '1993'
AND c.City IN ('Fremont', 'Portland');
------------------------------------------------------------

[Failure 55] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: In 1994 which title had less order quanty than the average order quantity? Find the title name, type and price.
BIRD Evidence: orders in 1994 refers to YEAR(ord_date) = 1994; order quantity refers to number of order expressed by ord_num; average order quantity = DIVIDE(SUM(ord_num), COUNT(title_id))
Gold DB: book_publishing_company | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: retails | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT p_name, p_type, p_retailprice
FROM part
JOIN lineitem ON part.p_partkey = lineitem.l_partkey
JOIN orders ON lineitem.l_orderkey = orders.o_orderkey
WHERE strftime('%Y', orders.o_orderdate) = '1994'
GROUP BY part.p_partkey
HAVING SUM(l_quantity) < (SELECT AVG(total_quantity) 
                         FROM (SELECT SUM(l_quantity) as total_quantity 
                               FROM lineitem 
                               JOIN orders ON lineitem.l_orderkey = orders.o_orderkey 
                               WHERE strftime('%Y', orders.o_orderdate) = '1994' 
                               GROUP BY l_partkey));

JOIN district d ON sd.District_ID = d.District_ID

[Failure 120] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    c.customer_first_name || ' ' || COALESCE(c.customer_middle_initial || ' ', '') || c.customer_last_name AS customer_name,

[Failure 134] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Find the university from which the professor who advised most undergraduate students graduated.
BIRD Evidence: university from which the professor graduated refers to graduate_from; undergraduate students refers to type = 'UG';
Gold DB: cs_semester | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: computer_student | Status: ERROR
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: WITH AdvisedCounts AS (
    SELECT a.p_id_dummy AS professor_id, COUNT(*) AS advised_count
    FROM advisedBy a
    JOIN person p ON a.p_id = p.p_id
    WHERE p.courseLevel = 'undergraduate'
    GROUP BY a.p_id_dummy
),
MaxAdvisedProfessor AS (
    SELECT professor_id
    FROM AdvisedCounts
    ORDER BY advised_count DESC
    LIMIT 1
)
SELECT p.university
FROM person p
JOIN MaxAdvisedProfessor m ON p.p_id = m.professor_id;

JOIN ProductModel pm ON pmdc.ProductModelID = pm.ProductModelID
JOIN Product p ON pm.ProductModelID = p.ProductModelID
JOIN SalesOrderDetail sod ON p.ProductID = sod.ProductID
JOIN SalesOrderHeader soh ON sod.SalesOrderID = soh.SalesOrderID
JOIN CurrencyRate cr ON soh.CurrencyRateID = cr.CurrencyRateID
JOIN Currency c ON cr.ToCurrencyCode = c.CurrencyCode
WHERE c.Name LIKE '%Euro%';
------------------------------------------------------------

[Failure 148] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What is the total price of items brought from ABC School Supply with a listed type of Other? Also include the list of the buyers' coordinates and school districts they belong to.
BIRD Evidence: ABC School Supply refer to vendor_name; listed type as Other refer to project_resource_type = 'Other'; coordinates refer to coordinates(school_latitude, school_longitude); total price of items refer to SUM(MULTIPLY(item_unit_price, item_quantity where vendor_name = ’ABC School Supply’))


Gold DB: donor | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customers_and_products_contacts | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    SUM(p.product_price * oi.order_quantity) AS total_price,
    a.line_1_number_building AS coordinates,
    a.state_province_county AS school_district
FROM 
    Products p
    JOIN Order_Items oi ON p.product_id = oi.product_id
    JOIN Customer_Orders co ON oi.order_id = co.order_id
    JOIN Customers c ON co.customer_id = c.customer_id
    JOIN Customer_Address_History cah ON c.customer_id = cah.customer_id
    JOIN Addresses a ON cah.address_id = a.address_id
WHERE 
    c.customer_name LIKE '%ABC School Supply%'
    AND p.product_type_code = 'Other'
    AND cah.date_to IS NULL
GROUP BY 
    a.line_1_number_building, a.state_province_county;

[Failure 152] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: For the Ligue 2 game that made the most goals, who is the winner of that game?
BIRD Evidence: Ligue 2 is the name of division; the most goals refer to MAX(SUM(FTHG, FTAG)) which are short names for Final-time Home-team Goals and Final-time Away-team Goals; winner refers to FTR = 'A';
Gold DB: european_football_1 | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: sports_competition | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT c.name
FROM competition_result cr
JOIN competition comp ON cr.Competition_ID = comp.Competition_ID
JOIN club c ON (
    CASE 
        WHEN CAST(SUBSTR(cr.Score, 1, INSTR(cr.Score, '-') - 1) AS INTEGER) > CAST(SUBSTR(cr.Score, INSTR(cr.Score, '-') + 1) AS INTEGER) 
        THEN cr.Club_ID_1 
        ELSE cr.Club_ID_2 
    END
) = c.Club_ID
WHERE comp.Competition_type LIKE '%Ligue 2%'
ORDER BY (
    CAST(SUBSTR(cr.Score, 1, INSTR(cr.Score, '-') - 1) AS INTEGER) + 
    CAST(SUBSTR(cr.Score, INSTR(cr.Score, '-') + 1) AS INTEGER)
) DESC
LIMIT 1;

[Failure 209] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: List the cast and the director of the movie with the id 1949144.
Gold DB: movielens | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: movies_4 | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    p.person_name,
    CASE 
        WHEN mc.movie_id IS NOT NULL THEN 'Cast'
        WHEN mc2.movie_id IS NOT NULL AND mc2.job LIKE '%Director%' THEN 'Director'
    END AS role
FROM person p
LEFT JOIN movie_cast mc ON p.person_id = mc.person_id AND mc.movie_id = 1949144
LEFT JOIN movie_crew mc2 ON p.person_id = mc2.person_id AND mc2.movie_id = 1949144 AND mc2.job LIKE '%Director%'
WHERE (mc.movie_id IS NOT NULL OR mc2.movie_id IS NOT NULL)
ORDER BY mc.cast_order;

[Failure 216] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Please list the team names which have at least 5 players were born in the same state.
BIRD Evidence: team name refers to teams.name; state that a player is born refers to birthState
Gold DB: professional_basketball | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: baseball_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT t.name
FROM team t
JOIN (
    SELECT a.team_id, p.birth_state
    FROM appearances a
    JOIN player p ON a.player_id = p.player_id
    WHERE p.birth_state IS NOT NULL
    GROUP BY a.team_id, p.birth_state
    HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT p.player_id) >= 5
) sub ON t.team_id = sub.team_id
GROUP BY t.name;

Selected DB: car_retails | Status: EMPTY_SET

Selected SQL: SELECT

    AVG(od.quantityOrdered) AS avg_ornaments_sold

JOIN 
    products p ON od.productCode = p.productCode

    AND strftime('%Y', o.orderDate) = '2018'

[Failure 223] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Find the percentage of products that were shipped from Burbank in 2018?
BIRD Evidence: DIVIDE(SUM(Order Quantity where City Name = 'Burbank' and SUBSTR(OrderDate, -2) = '18')), (SUM(Order Quantity where SUBSTR(OrderDate, -2) = '18')) as percentage;
Gold DB: regional_sales | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: e_commerce | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN s.shipment_date LIKE '2018%' AND c.town_city = 'Burbank' THEN p.product_id END) * 100.0 / 
    COUNT(DISTINCT p.product_id)) AS percentage_shipped_from_burbank_2018
FROM Products p
LEFT JOIN Order_Items oi ON p.product_id = oi.product_id
LEFT JOIN Shipment_Items si ON oi.order_item_id = si.order_item_id
LEFT JOIN Shipments s ON si.shipment_id = s.shipment_id
LEFT JOIN Orders o ON s.order_id = o.order_id
LEFT JOIN Customers c ON o.customer_id = c.customer_id;

[Failure 230] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Selected SQL: SELECT AVG(order_count)

[Failure 231] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Calculate the average monthly order and percentage of warehouse "WARE-NMK1003" in 2019. Among them, mention number of orders for floor lamps.
BIRD Evidence: "WARE-NMK1003" is the WarehouseCode; in 2019 refers to SUBSTR(OrderDate, -2) = '19'; average = Divide (Count (OrderNumber where SUBSTR(OrderDate, -2) = '19'), 12); Percentage = Divide (Count(OrderNumber where WarehouseCode = 'WARE-NMK1003'), Count(OrderNumber)) * 100; 'Floor Lamps' is the Product Name; number of orders refers to Count(OrderNumber)
Gold DB: regional_sales | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: department_store | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: WITH MonthlyOrders AS (
    SELECT 
        strftime('%Y-%m', co.order_date) AS month,
        COUNT(*) AS total_orders,
        COUNT(CASE WHEN p.product_name LIKE '%floor lamp%' THEN 1 END) AS floor_lamp_orders
    FROM Customer_Orders co
    JOIN Order_Items oi ON co.order_id = oi.order_id
    JOIN Products p ON oi.product_id = p.product_id
    JOIN Departments d ON oi.order_id IS NOT NULL
    JOIN Department_Stores ds ON d.dept_store_id = ds.dept_store_id
    WHERE ds.store_name = 'WARE-NMK1003'
    AND co.order_date BETWEEN '2019-01-01' AND '2019-12-31'
    GROUP BY strftime('%Y-%m', co.order_date)
)
SELECT 
    AVG(total_orders) AS avg_monthly_orders,
    (SUM(floor_lamp_orders) * 100.0 / SUM(total_orders)) AS floor_lamp_percentage,
    SUM(floor_lamp_orders) AS total_floor_lamp_orders
FROM MonthlyOrders;

[Failure 235] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Selected DB: car_retails | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    p.productCode,

[Failure 240] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Gold DB: regional_sales | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customer_deliveries | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT c.customer_id)
FROM Customers c
JOIN Regular_Orders ro ON c.customer_id = ro.distributer_id

        SELECT AVG(order_count)
        FROM (

            FROM Regular_Orders
            GROUP BY distributer_id
        )
    )
);

[Failure 256] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What is the detailed coordinates of the store where the product with the 4th highest profit were purchased from?
BIRD Evidence: detailed coordinates refers to Latitude, Longitude; highest net profit = Max(Subtract(Unit Price, Unit Cost))
Gold DB: regional_sales | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: retail_world | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: WITH ProductProfit AS (
    SELECT 
        p.ProductID,
        p.ProductName,
        SUM(od.Quantity * p.Price) AS TotalProfit
    FROM Products p
    JOIN OrderDetails od ON p.ProductID = od.ProductID
    GROUP BY p.ProductID, p.ProductName
    ORDER BY TotalProfit DESC
    LIMIT 4
),
FourthHighestProduct AS (
    SELECT ProductID FROM ProductProfit ORDER BY TotalProfit ASC LIMIT 1
),
OrderWithProduct AS (
    SELECT DISTINCT o.OrderID, o.ShipperID
    FROM Orders o
    JOIN OrderDetails od ON o.OrderID = od.OrderID
    WHERE od.ProductID = (SELECT ProductID FROM FourthHighestProduct)
),
StoreCoordinates AS (
    SELECT 
        s.ShipperID,
        s.ShipperName AS StoreName,
        s.Phone AS Coordinates
    FROM Shippers s
    WHERE s.ShipperID IN (SELECT ShipperID FROM OrderWithProduct)
)
SELECT * FROM StoreCoordinates;

[Failure 257] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Between 2018 to 2020, what is the average amount of shipped orders per year under Carl Nguyen?
BIRD Evidence: shipped refers to ShipDate; between 2018 and 2020 refers to SUBSTR(ShipDate, -2) IN ('18', '19', '20'); 'Carl Nguyen' is the name of Sales Team; average shipped orders per year = Divide (Count(OrderNumber), 3)
Gold DB: regional_sales | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: works_cycles | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    strftime('%Y', soh.ShipDate) AS Year,
    COUNT(*) AS ShippedOrders
FROM 
    SalesOrderHeader soh
JOIN 
    SalesPerson sp ON soh.SalesPersonID = sp.BusinessEntityID
JOIN 
    Employee e ON sp.BusinessEntityID = e.BusinessEntityID
JOIN 
    Person p ON e.BusinessEntityID = p.BusinessEntityID
WHERE 
    p.FirstName LIKE 'Carl' 
    AND p.LastName LIKE 'Nguyen'
    AND soh.ShipDate IS NOT NULL
    AND soh.ShipDate BETWEEN '2018-01-01' AND '2020-12-31'
GROUP BY 
    strftime('%Y', soh.ShipDate);

[Failure 258] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Selected SQL: WITH ProductProfit AS (
    SELECT 
        p.product_id,
        p.product_name,
        (p.typical_selling_price - p.typical_buying_price) AS net_profit,

LIMIT 1;

[Failure 266] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Compute the average time in minute for each age group
BIRD Evidence: teenager refers to 13 < age < = 19; adult refers to 19 < age < = 65; elder refers to age < = 65; highest average time per complaint = max(divide(sum(ser_time), count(ser_time)))
Gold DB: retail_complains | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: vehicle_rent | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    CASE 
        WHEN c.age < 20 THEN 'Under 20'
        WHEN c.age BETWEEN 20 AND 29 THEN '20-29'
        WHEN c.age BETWEEN 30 AND 39 THEN '30-39'
        WHEN c.age BETWEEN 40 AND 49 THEN '40-49'
        WHEN c.age BETWEEN 50 AND 59 THEN '50-59'
        ELSE '60+'
    END AS age_group,
    AVG(rh.total_hours * 60) AS average_time_minutes
FROM Renting_history rh
JOIN Customers c ON rh.customer_id = c.id
GROUP BY age_group;

[Failure 282] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Which of the American customers have experienced a delay in the shipment and how long was the longest?
BIRD Evidence: "American" refers to Country = 'USA'; longest delay in shipment refers to Max(Subtract(RequiredDate, ShippedDate)); customer refers to CustomerID
Gold DB: retail_world | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: e_commerce | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT c.customer_id, c.customer_first_name, c.customer_last_name, MAX(julianday(s.shipment_date) - julianday(o.date_order_placed)) AS max_delay_days
FROM Customers c
JOIN Orders o ON c.customer_id = o.customer_id
JOIN Shipments s ON o.order_id = s.order_id
WHERE c.country = 'USA'
AND s.shipment_date > o.date_order_placed
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.customer_first_name, c.customer_last_name
HAVING max_delay_days > 0;

Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT c.customer_first_name || ' ' || COALESCE(c.customer_middle_initial || ' ', '') || c.customer_last_name AS contact_name, c.phone_number

GROUP BY c.customer_id

LIMIT 1;

[Failure 288] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What percentage of orders were placed by customers in Madrid city in 1996?
BIRD Evidence: "Madrid" is the City; in 1996 refers to YEAR (OrderDate) = 1996; percentage = Divide (Count (CustomerID where City = 'Madrid'), Count (CustomerID)) * 100
Gold DB: retail_world | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customers_and_invoices | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN c.town_city = 'Madrid' AND strftime('%Y', o.date_order_placed) = '1996' THEN o.order_id END) * 100.0 / 
     COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN strftime('%Y', o.date_order_placed) = '1996' THEN o.order_id END)) AS percentage
FROM Orders o
JOIN Customers c ON o.customer_id = c.customer_id;

[Failure 297] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What is the monthly average number of products shipped via Federal Shipping for the year 1996?
BIRD Evidence: monthly average number of products refers to DIVIDE(SUM(OrderID), 12); shipped via Federal Shipping refers to CompanyName = 'Federal Shipping'; for the year 1996 refers to year(ShippedDate) = 1996
Gold DB: retail_world | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: e_commerce | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    strftime('%Y-%m', s.shipment_date) AS month,
    COUNT(*) / COUNT(DISTINCT strftime('%Y-%m', s.shipment_date)) AS avg_products_shipped
FROM 
    Shipments s
JOIN 
    Shipment_Items si ON s.shipment_id = si.shipment_id
WHERE 
    s.shipment_tracking_number LIKE '%Federal Shipping%'
    AND strftime('%Y', s.shipment_date) = '1996'
GROUP BY 
    month;

[Failure 311] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Selected SQL: SELECT p.productCode, p.productName, p.productLine, p.productScale, p.productVendor, p.productDescription, p.quantityInStock, p.buyPrice, p.MSRP

[Failure 344] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Among the employees who handled orders to Brazil, who has the highest salary and calculate the average salary of them.
BIRD Evidence: orders to Brazil refers to ShipCountry = 'Brazil'; highest salary refers to max(salary); average salary = AVG(Salary)
Gold DB: retail_world | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: works_cycles | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    e.BusinessEntityID,
    p.FirstName || ' ' || p.LastName AS EmployeeName,
    MAX(eph.Rate) AS HighestSalary,
    AVG(eph.Rate) AS AverageSalary
FROM 
    Employee e
JOIN 
    Person p ON e.BusinessEntityID = p.BusinessEntityID
JOIN 
    EmployeePayHistory eph ON e.BusinessEntityID = eph.BusinessEntityID
JOIN 
    SalesPerson sp ON e.BusinessEntityID = sp.BusinessEntityID
JOIN 
    SalesOrderHeader soh ON sp.BusinessEntityID = soh.SalesPersonID
JOIN 
    Customer c ON soh.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
JOIN 
    SalesTerritory st ON c.TerritoryID = st.TerritoryID
JOIN 
    CountryRegion cr ON st.CountryRegionCode = cr.CountryRegionCode
WHERE 
    cr.Name = 'Brazil'
GROUP BY 
    e.BusinessEntityID, EmployeeName
ORDER BY 
    HighestSalary DESC
LIMIT 1;

Query: List the full name of customers who spend more than 50,000 in descending order the amount spend.
BIRD Evidence: full name of the customer = FirstName, MiddleInitial, LastName; more than 50,000 in the amount refers to MULTIPLY(Quantity, Price) > 50000;
Gold DB: sales | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customers_and_orders | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    c.customer_name,
    SUM(p.product_price * oi.order_quantity) AS total_spent
FROM 
    Customers c
    JOIN Customer_Orders co ON c.customer_id = co.customer_id
    JOIN Order_Items oi ON co.order_id = oi.order_id
    JOIN Products p ON oi.product_id = p.product_id
GROUP BY 
    c.customer_id, c.customer_name
HAVING 
    SUM(p.product_price * oi.order_quantity) > 50000
ORDER BY 
    total_spent DESC;
------------------------------------------------------------

[Failure 390] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: What is the most popular size of t-shirt ordered by the club members?
BIRD Evidence: most popular size of t-shirt ordered refers to MAX(COUNT(t_shirt_size))
Gold DB: student_club | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: club_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT t_shirt_size, COUNT(*) AS count
FROM (
    SELECT 
        CASE 
            WHEN Age < 20 THEN 'Small'
            WHEN Age BETWEEN 20 AND 22 THEN 'Medium'
            WHEN Age > 22 THEN 'Large'
        END AS t_shirt_size
    FROM Student s
    JOIN Member_of_club m ON s.StuID = m.StuID
)
GROUP BY t_shirt_size
ORDER BY count DESC
LIMIT 1;

[Failure 407] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Please list any three orders that caused a loss to the company.
BIRD Evidence: caused a loss to the company refers to Profit < 0
Gold DB: superstore | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customers_and_invoices | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: SELECT o.order_id, o.customer_id, o.date_order_placed, SUM(ili.derived_total_cost - (ili.product_quantity * p.unit_price)) AS total_loss
FROM Orders o
JOIN Order_Items oi ON o.order_id = oi.order_id
JOIN Products p ON oi.product_id = p.product_id
JOIN Invoice_Line_Items ili ON oi.order_item_id = ili.order_item_id
GROUP BY o.order_id
HAVING total_loss < 0
LIMIT 3;

[Failure 416] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

[Failure 417] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop
Query: Among the vendors with maximum orders betweeen 500 to 750, which vendor has the 10th highest profit on net?
BIRD Evidence: maximum orders refers to MaxOrderQty; MaxOrderQty BETWEEN '500' AND '750'; profit on net = SUBTRACT(LastReceiptCost, StandardPrice);
Gold DB: works_cycles | Status: MISSING
Selected DB: customers_and_products_contacts | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: N/A
Selected SQL: WITH VendorOrders AS (
    SELECT 
        c.customer_id,
        c.customer_name AS vendor_name,
        COUNT(DISTINCT co.order_id) AS total_orders
    FROM Customers c
    JOIN Customer_Orders co ON c.customer_id = co.customer_id
    GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.customer_name
    HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT co.order_id) BETWEEN 500 AND 750
),
VendorProfits AS (
    SELECT 
        vo.vendor_name,
        SUM(oi.order_quantity * p.product_price) AS total_profit,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY SUM(oi.order_quantity * p.product_price) DESC) AS profit_rank
    FROM VendorOrders vo
    JOIN Customer_Orders co ON vo.customer_id = co.customer_id
    JOIN Order_Items oi ON co.order_id = oi.order_id
    JOIN Products p ON oi.product_id = p.product_id
    GROUP BY vo.vendor_name
)
SELECT vendor_name
FROM VendorProfits
WHERE profit_rank = 10;

[Failure 420] - CATEGORY: Retrieval Funnel Drop

Selected SQL: SELECT p.product_name, SUM(ili.derived_total_cost - ili.derived_product_cost) AS total_profit

[Failure 496] - CATEGORY: SQL Generator Choke
Query: Which of the top 3 economies by GDP has the lowest proportion of the economy devoted to agriculture?
BIRD Evidence: Economies refers to countries
Gold DB: mondial_geo | Status: ERROR
Selected DB: world_development_indicators | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: SELECT e.Country
FROM economy e
ORDER BY e.GDP DESC
LIMIT 3
ORDER BY e.Agriculture ASC
LIMIT 1;
Selected SQL: WITH GDPData AS (
    SELECT 
        i.CountryCode,
        i.Value AS GDP,
        i.Year
    FROM Indicators i
    WHERE i.IndicatorCode LIKE '%GDP%' 
      AND i.Year = (SELECT MAX(Year) FROM Indicators WHERE IndicatorCode LIKE '%GDP%')
    ORDER BY i.Value DESC
    LIMIT 3
),
AgricultureData AS (
    SELECT 
        i.CountryCode,
        i.Value AS AgricultureValue,
        i.Year
    FROM Indicators i
    WHERE i.IndicatorCode LIKE '%agriculture%value added%GDP%'
      AND i.Year = (SELECT MAX(Year) FROM Indicators WHERE IndicatorCode LIKE '%agriculture%value added%GDP%')
)
SELECT 
    c.ShortName AS Country,
    g.GDP,
    a.AgricultureValue AS AgriculturePercentage
FROM GDPData g
JOIN Country c ON g.CountryCode = c.CountryCode
JOIN AgricultureData a ON g.CountryCode = a.CountryCode
ORDER BY a.AgricultureValue ASC
LIMIT 1;

[Failure 511] - CATEGORY: SQL Generator Choke
Query: How much more is the Florida store's computer product unit price than the Texas store?
BIRD Evidence: "Florida" and "Texas" are both the name of State; Computer product refers to Product Name = 'Computers; difference in unit price = Subtract (Unit Price where State = 'Florida', Unit Price where State = 'Texas')
Gold DB: regional_sales | Status: ERROR
Selected DB: retail_complains | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    (SELECT p.UnitPrice FROM Products p 
     JOIN Customers c ON p.ProductID = c.ProductID 
     JOIN Regions r ON c.StateCode = r.StateCode 
     WHERE r.State = 'Florida' AND p.ProductName LIKE '%computer%') - 
    (SELECT p.UnitPrice FROM Products p 
     JOIN Customers c ON p.ProductID = c.ProductID 
     JOIN Regions r ON c.StateCode = r.StateCode 
     WHERE r.State = 'Texas' AND p.ProductName LIKE '%computer%') 
AS PriceDifference;
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (florida_price.avg_price - texas_price.avg_price) AS price_difference
FROM 
    (SELECT AVG(CAST(SUBSTR(r.Reviews, INSTR(r.Reviews, '$') + 1) AS REAL)) AS avg_price
     FROM reviews r
     JOIN district d ON r.district_id = d.district_id
     JOIN state s ON d.state_abbrev = s.StateCode
     WHERE s.State = 'Florida' AND r.Product LIKE '%computer%') AS florida_price,
    (SELECT AVG(CAST(SUBSTR(r.Reviews, INSTR(r.Reviews, '$') + 1) AS REAL)) AS avg_price
     FROM reviews r
     JOIN district d ON r.district_id = d.district_id
     JOIN state s ON d.state_abbrev = s.StateCode
     WHERE s.State = 'Texas' AND r.Product LIKE '%computer%') AS texas_price;

[Failure 513] - CATEGORY: SQL Generator Choke

Gold SQL: SELECT c."Customer Names"

    SELECT CustomerID
    FROM Products p

        SELECT ProductID, MAX("Net Profit") as MaxProfit
        FROM Products
    ) mp ON p.ProductID = mp.ProductID
) high_profit ON c.CustomerID = high_profit.CustomerID;

    FROM Invoice_Line_Items ili2

)
LIMIT 1;

[Failure 518] - CATEGORY: SQL Generator Choke
Query: Who is the sales representative of the customer who has made the highest payment? Include the full name of employee and his/her supervisor.
BIRD Evidence: highest payment refers to Max(Multiply(Quantity, UnitPrice, Subtract(1, Discount))); full name refers to FirstName, LastName; his/her supervisor refers to 'ReportsTo'
Gold DB: retail_world | Status: ERROR
Selected DB: car_retails | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    e.FirstName || ' ' || e.LastName AS EmployeeName,
    sup.FirstName || ' ' || sup.LastName AS SupervisorName
FROM Orders o
JOIN Customers c ON o.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
JOIN Employees e ON o.EmployeeID = e.EmployeeID
LEFT JOIN Employees sup ON e.ReportsTo = sup.EmployeeID
JOIN (
    SELECT 
        o.CustomerID,
        SUM(od.Quantity * p.Price) AS TotalPayment
    FROM Orders o
    JOIN OrderDetails od ON o.OrderID = od.OrderID
    JOIN Products p ON od.ProductID = p.ProductID
    GROUP BY o.CustomerID
    ORDER BY TotalPayment DESC
    LIMIT 1
) highest_paying_customer ON o.CustomerID = highest_paying_customer.CustomerID
LIMIT 1;
Selected SQL: SELECT e.firstName || ' ' || e.lastName AS salesRepName, s.firstName || ' ' || s.lastName AS supervisorName
FROM employees e
JOIN employees s ON e.reportsTo = s.employeeNumber
WHERE e.employeeNumber = (
    SELECT c.salesRepEmployeeNumber
    FROM customers c
    JOIN payments p ON c.customerNumber = p.customerNumber
    GROUP BY c.customerNumber
    ORDER BY SUM(p.amount) DESC
    LIMIT 1
);

    GROUP BY o.OrderID
),
SubordinateCount AS (
    SELECT COUNT(*) AS SubordinateCount
    FROM Employees
    WHERE ReportsTo = 2
)

    SubordinateCount.SubordinateCount,
    MAX(SubordinateOrders.OrderValue) AS MaxOrderValue
FROM SubordinateCount, SubordinateOrders;

    MAX(i.Total) AS biggest_order_value
FROM Employee e
JOIN Customer c ON c.SupportRepId = e.EmployeeId

WHERE e.ReportsTo = 2;

    SELECT ID 
    FROM Laboratory 
    WHERE IgM NOT BETWEEN (SELECT AVG(IgM) - 2*STDEV(IgM) FROM Laboratory) 
                       AND (SELECT AVG(IgM) + 2*STDEV(IgM) FROM Laboratory)
) 
GROUP BY Diagnosis 
ORDER BY count DESC 
LIMIT 1;
Selected SQL: SELECT c.DESCRIPTION 
FROM observations o
JOIN conditions c ON o.PATIENT = c.PATIENT
WHERE o.DESCRIPTION LIKE '%Ig M%' AND o.VALUE != 'normal'
GROUP BY c.DESCRIPTION
ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC
LIMIT 1;

[Failure 608] - CATEGORY: The "Empty Set" Trap
Query: What's the decrease rate of the game plays did David Aebischer after he got traded in 2005?
BIRD Evidence: DIVIDE(SUBTRACT(SUM(GP(year = 2005), SUM(GP(year = 2006)), SUM(GP(year = 2005)) as percentage;
Gold DB: hockey | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Selected DB: ice_hockey_draft | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Goalies WHERE playerID = (SELECT playerID FROM Master WHERE firstName LIKE 'David' AND lastName LIKE 'Aebischer') AND year < 2005) - 
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM Goalies WHERE playerID = (SELECT playerID FROM Master WHERE firstName LIKE 'David' AND lastName LIKE 'Aebischer') AND year >= 2005) 
AS decrease_rate;
Selected SQL: WITH trades AS (
    SELECT 
        s1.ELITEID,
        s1.SEASON,
        s1.TEAM,
        s1.LEAGUE,
        s1.GP,
        LAG(s1.TEAM) OVER (PARTITION BY s1.ELITEID ORDER BY s1.SEASON) as prev_team
    FROM SeasonStatus s1
    JOIN PlayerInfo p ON s1.ELITEID = p.ELITEID
    WHERE p.PlayerName LIKE '%David Aebischer%'
),
trade_season AS (
    SELECT 
        ELITEID,
        SEASON as trade_season,
        TEAM as new_team,
        prev_team as old_team,
        GP as post_trade_gp
    FROM trades
    WHERE TEAM != prev_team AND SEASON = 2005
),
pre_trade_gp AS (
    SELECT 
        t.ELITEID,
        SUM(s.GP) as total_pre_trade_gp
    FROM trade_season t
    JOIN SeasonStatus s ON t.ELITEID = s.ELITEID
    WHERE s.SEASON < t.trade_season
    GROUP BY t.ELITEID
),
post_trade_gp AS (
    SELECT 
        t.ELITEID,
        SUM(s.GP) as total_post_trade_gp
    FROM trade_season t
    JOIN SeasonStatus s ON t.ELITEID = s.ELITEID
    WHERE s.SEASON >= t.trade_season
    GROUP BY t.ELITEID
)
SELECT 
    (pre.total_pre_trade_gp - post.total_post_trade_gp) * 100.0 / pre.total_pre_trade_gp as decrease_rate
FROM pre_trade_gp pre

[Failure 622] - CATEGORY: The "Empty Set" Trap
Query: What is the capital of the 3rd most populated country in Asia and what is the capital city's ratio in percentage (%) against the overall population of the country?
Gold DB: mondial_geo | Status: EMPTY_SET
Selected DB: world_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: WITH RankedCountries AS (
    SELECT 
        c.Name AS Country, 
        c.Capital,
        c.Population AS CountryPopulation,
        city.Population AS CapitalPopulation,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY e.Continent ORDER BY c.Population DESC) AS PopulationRank
    FROM 
        country c
    JOIN 
        encompasses e ON c.Name = e.Country
    JOIN 
        city ON c.Capital = city.Name AND c.Name = city.Country
    WHERE 
        e.Continent = 'Asia'
)
SELECT 
    Country, 
    Capital, 
    ROUND((CapitalPopulation * 100.0 / CountryPopulation), 2) AS CapitalPercentage
FROM 
    RankedCountries
WHERE 
    PopulationRank = 3;
Selected SQL: WITH ranked_countries AS (
    SELECT 
        c.Code,
        c.Name,
        c.Population,
        c.Capital
    FROM country c
    WHERE c.Continent = 'Asia'
    ORDER BY c.Population DESC
    LIMIT 3
),
third_country AS (
    SELECT 
        Code,
        Name,
        Population AS country_population,
        Capital
    FROM ranked_countries
    ORDER BY Population ASC
    LIMIT 1
)
SELECT 
    city.Name AS capital_name,
    (city.Population * 100.0 / tc.country_population) AS capital_ratio_percentage
FROM third_country tc
JOIN city ON tc.Capital = city.ID;

[Failure 655] - CATEGORY: The "Empty Set" Trap
Query: What is the proportion of action movies directors who are called 'box office success paradox'?
BIRD Evidence: 'box office success paradox' means average revenue exceeds their quality; The proportion can be computed by [(avg_revenue > d_quality) / ()] * 100%
Gold DB: movielens | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Selected DB: movie | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    CAST(COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN m2d.genre = 'Action' AND d.d_quality = 'box office success paradox' THEN m2d.directorid END) AS REAL) / 
    NULLIF(COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN m2d.genre = 'Action' THEN m2d.directorid END), 0)
FROM movies2directors m2d
JOIN directors d ON m2d.directorid = d.directorid;
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN m.Genre LIKE '%Action%' AND m.Gross > m.Budget THEN m.MovieID END) * 1.0 / 
     COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN m.Genre LIKE '%Action%' THEN m.MovieID END)) AS proportion
FROM movie m
WHERE m.Genre LIKE '%Action%';

[Failure 662] - CATEGORY: The "Empty Set" Trap
Query: What is the average ratio between female and male actors in a movie?
BIRD Evidence: female refers to gender = 'Female'；male refers to gender = 'Male'; average ratio = divide(divide(sum(gender_id) when gender = 'Female', sum(gender_id) when gender = 'Male'), count(movie_id)) as percentage
Gold DB: movies_4 | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Selected DB: movielens | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: WITH movie_gender_counts AS (
    SELECT 
        mc.movie_id,
        SUM(CASE WHEN g.gender = 'female' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS female_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN g.gender = 'male' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS male_count
    FROM movie_cast mc
    JOIN gender g ON mc.gender_id = g.gender_id
    WHERE g.gender IN ('female', 'male')
    GROUP BY mc.movie_id
    HAVING male_count > 0
)
SELECT AVG(1.0 * female_count / male_count) AS avg_female_male_ratio
FROM movie_gender_counts;
Selected SQL: WITH actor_counts AS (
    SELECT 
        m.movieid,
        COUNT(CASE WHEN a.a_gender = 'F' THEN 1 END) AS female_count,
        COUNT(CASE WHEN a.a_gender = 'M' THEN 1 END) AS male_count
    FROM movies m
    JOIN movies2actors ma ON m.movieid = ma.movieid
    JOIN actors a ON ma.actorid = a.actorid
    GROUP BY m.movieid
    HAVING male_count > 0
)
SELECT AVG(1.0 * female_count / male_count) AS avg_ratio
FROM actor_counts;

Gold DB: professional_basketball | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Selected DB: hockey | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT pt.playerID)
FROM players_teams pt

[Failure 666] - CATEGORY: The "Empty Set" Trap
Query: State the name of teams ranked first five or more times and lost a league two or more times between 1980 and 2000?
BIRD Evidence: name of team refers to teams.name; between 1980 and 2000 refers to year between 1980 and 2000; ranked first five or more times refers to count(rank = 1) > = 5; lost a league two or more times refers to lost > 2
Gold DB: professional_basketball | Status: EMPTY_SET
Selected DB: hockey | Status: EMPTY_SET
Gold SQL: SELECT t.name
FROM teams t
WHERE t.year BETWEEN 1980 AND 2000
GROUP BY t.tmID, t.name
HAVING COUNT(CASE WHEN t.rank = 1 THEN 1 END) >= 5
   AND COUNT(CASE WHEN t.lgID = 'lost' THEN 1 END) >= 2;
Selected SQL: SELECT t.name
FROM Teams t
JOIN (
    SELECT tmID, COUNT(*) AS first_place_count
    FROM Teams
    WHERE year BETWEEN 1980 AND 2000 AND rank = 1
    GROUP BY tmID
    HAVING COUNT(*) >= 5
) r1 ON t.tmID = r1.tmID
JOIN (
    SELECT tmID, COUNT(*) AS league_loss_count
    FROM Teams
    WHERE year BETWEEN 1980 AND 2000 AND lgID = 'L' AND playoff = 'N'
    GROUP BY tmID
    HAVING COUNT(*) >= 2
) r2 ON t.tmID = r2.tmID
GROUP BY t.tmID, t.name;

[Failure 669] - CATEGORY: The "Empty Set" Trap
Query: Among all the users with the average ratings of at least 4 and above of all reviews, calculate the percent that have no fans or followers.
BIRD Evidence: average ratings of at least 4 refers to user_average_stars > = 4; no fans or followers refers to user_fans = 'None'; percentage = divide(count(user_id where user_average_stars > = 4 and user_fans = 'None'), sum(user_id where user_average_stars > = 4))*100%
Gold DB: public_review_platform | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Selected DB: yelp | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    ROUND(100.0 * SUM(CASE WHEN u.user_fans = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) / COUNT(*), 2) AS percentage_no_fans
FROM Users u
WHERE u.user_average_stars >= 4;
Selected SQL: WITH UserAvgRating AS (
    SELECT 
        u.uid,
        u.user_id,
        AVG(r.rating) AS avg_rating
    FROM user u
    JOIN review r ON u.user_id = r.user_id
    GROUP BY u.uid, u.user_id
    HAVING AVG(r.rating) >= 4
),
UserFans AS (
    SELECT 
        uar.user_id,
        COUNT(*) AS fan_count
    FROM UserAvgRating uar
    LEFT JOIN user u ON uar.user_id = u.user_id
    WHERE u.user_id IS NOT NULL
    GROUP BY uar.user_id
    HAVING COUNT(*) = 0
)
SELECT 
    (COUNT(DISTINCT uf.user_id) * 100.0 / COUNT(DISTINCT uar.user_id)) AS percent_no_fans
FROM UserAvgRating uar
LEFT JOIN UserFans uf ON uar.user_id = uf.user_id;

Query: Among the teenager clients who use Google account and Microsoft account, which group of client is more than the other?
BIRD Evidence: teenager refers to 13 < age < = 19; Google account refers to email like '%@gmail.com'; Microsoft account refers to email like '%@outlook.com'
Gold DB: retail_complains | Status: EMPTY_SET
Selected DB: e_government | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    CASE 
        WHEN e.Product LIKE '%Google%' THEN 'Google'
        WHEN e.Product LIKE '%Microsoft%' THEN 'Microsoft'
    END AS account_type,
    COUNT(DISTINCT c.client_id) AS client_count
FROM client c
JOIN events e ON c.client_id = e.Client_ID
WHERE c.age BETWEEN 13 AND 19
  AND (e.Product LIKE '%Google%' OR e.Product LIKE '%Microsoft%')
GROUP BY account_type
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT c.client_id) > 0
ORDER BY client_count DESC
LIMIT 1;
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    CASE 
        WHEN COUNT(CASE WHEN i.individual_email LIKE '%@gmail.com%' THEN 1 END) > COUNT(CASE WHEN i.individual_email LIKE '%@outlook.com%' OR i.individual_email LIKE '%@hotmail.com%' THEN 1 END) 
        THEN 'Google account users'
        ELSE 'Microsoft account users'
    END AS larger_group
FROM Individuals i
JOIN Parties p ON i.individual_id = p.party_id
WHERE i.individual_email LIKE '%@gmail.com%' 
   OR i.individual_email LIKE '%@outlook.com%' 
   OR i.individual_email LIKE '%@hotmail.com%';
------------------------------------------------------------

Gold DB: retail_complains | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Selected DB: financial | Status: ZERO_COUNT
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    (COUNT(CASE WHEN c.sex = 'Female' THEN 1 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*)) AS percentage_female
FROM 
    client c
JOIN 
    district d ON c.district_id = d.district_id
JOIN 
    state s ON d.state_abbrev = s.StateCode
WHERE 
    s.Region = 'Middle Atlantic';
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (COUNT(*) * 100.0 / (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM client WHERE district_id IN (SELECT district_id FROM district WHERE A3 = 'Middle Atlantic'))) 
FROM client 
WHERE gender = 'F' AND district_id IN (SELECT district_id FROM district WHERE A3 = 'Middle Atlantic');

[Failure 734] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error
Query: Name the paper which is cited most times and the paper which is cited least times? Also, find the number of times each one is cited.
Gold DB: citeseer | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: aan_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: WITH citation_counts AS (
    SELECT 
        cited_paper_id,
        COUNT(*) AS citation_count
    FROM cites
    GROUP BY cited_paper_id
),
max_citation AS (
    SELECT cited_paper_id, citation_count
    FROM citation_counts
    ORDER BY citation_count DESC
    LIMIT 1
),
min_citation AS (
    SELECT cited_paper_id, citation_count
    FROM citation_counts
    ORDER BY citation_count ASC
    LIMIT 1
)
SELECT 
    'Most cited' AS type,
    m.cited_paper_id AS paper_id,
    m.citation_count AS times_cited
FROM max_citation m
UNION ALL
SELECT 
    'Least cited' AS type,
    mi.cited_paper_id AS paper_id,
    mi.citation_count AS times_cited
FROM min_citation mi;
Selected SQL: WITH CitationCounts AS (
    SELECT cited_paper_id AS paper_id, COUNT(*) AS citation_count
    FROM Citation
    GROUP BY cited_paper_id
),
MaxCitation AS (
    SELECT paper_id, citation_count
    FROM CitationCounts
    ORDER BY citation_count DESC
    LIMIT 1
),
MinCitation AS (
    SELECT paper_id, citation_count
    FROM CitationCounts
    ORDER BY citation_count ASC
    LIMIT 1
)
SELECT p.paper_id, p.title, 'Most Cited' AS citation_type, m.citation_count
FROM Paper p
JOIN MaxCitation m ON p.paper_id = m.paper_id
UNION ALL
SELECT p.paper_id, p.title, 'Least Cited' AS citation_type, mi.citation_count
FROM Paper p
JOIN MinCitation mi ON p.paper_id = mi.paper_id;

[Failure 758] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error
Query: Which position has won the most awards and who is the most recent player that was awarded with an award in that position? Indicate the name of the award and the full name of the player.
BIRD Evidence: position has won the most awards refers to pos(max(count(award))); most recent player refers to playerID(pos(max(count(award)))& max(year)); full name = nameGiven + lastName
Gold DB: hockey | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: baseball_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    ap.pos,
    COUNT(*) AS award_count,
    m.firstName || ' ' || m.lastName AS player_name,
    ap.award,
    ap.year
FROM 
    AwardsPlayers ap
JOIN 
    Master m ON ap.playerID = m.playerID
WHERE 
    ap.year = (
        SELECT MAX(ap2.year) 
        FROM AwardsPlayers ap2 
        WHERE ap2.pos = ap.pos
    )
GROUP BY 
    ap.pos
ORDER BY 
    award_count DESC
LIMIT 1;
Selected SQL: WITH PositionAwards AS (
    SELECT 
        f.pos,
        COUNT(*) AS award_count
    FROM 
        player_award pa
    JOIN 
        fielding f ON pa.player_id = f.player_id AND pa.year = f.year
    GROUP BY 
        f.pos
    ORDER BY 
        award_count DESC
    LIMIT 1
),
MostRecentAward AS (
    SELECT 
        f.pos,
        pa.award_id,
        pa.year,
        pa.player_id,
        p.name_first,
        p.name_last,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY f.pos ORDER BY pa.year DESC) as rn
    FROM 
        player_award pa
    JOIN 
        fielding f ON pa.player_id = f.player_id AND pa.year = f.year
    JOIN 
        player p ON pa.player_id = p.player_id
    WHERE 
        f.pos = (SELECT pos FROM PositionAwards)
)
SELECT 
    mra.pos,
    mra.award_id,
    mra.name_first || ' ' || mra.name_last AS player_name
FROM 
    MostRecentAward mra
WHERE 
    mra.rn = 1;

[Failure 764] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error

WHERE t.year = 2000
GROUP BY t.team_id, p.birth_country
HAVING t.w * 1.0 / (t.w + t.l) = (
    SELECT MAX(w * 1.0 / (w + l))
    FROM team
    WHERE year = 2000 AND w + l > 0
)
ORDER BY player_count DESC;

[Failure 772] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error
Query: Of all the countries in which English is spoken, what percentage has English as their only language?
BIRD Evidence: Percentage = [count(countries 100% English) / count(countries English)] * 100%
Gold DB: mondial_geo | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: country_language | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: WITH english_only_countries AS (
    SELECT Country
    FROM language
    WHERE Name LIKE 'English'
    GROUP BY Country
    HAVING COUNT(*) = 1
),
total_english_countries AS (
    SELECT DISTINCT Country
    FROM language
    WHERE Name LIKE 'English'
)
SELECT 
    (COUNT(*) * 100.0 / (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM total_english_countries)) AS percentage
FROM english_only_countries;
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (COUNT(*) * 100.0 / (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT c.id) 
                         FROM countries c 
                         JOIN official_languages ol ON c.id = ol.country_id 
                         JOIN languages l ON ol.language_id = l.id 
                         WHERE l.name LIKE '%English%')) 
FROM countries c 
WHERE c.id IN (
    SELECT country_id 
    FROM official_languages 
    GROUP BY country_id 
    HAVING COUNT(*) = 1 
    AND MAX(language_id) IN (SELECT id FROM languages WHERE name LIKE '%English%')
);

[Failure 806] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error
Query: How many titles did Mary Smith rent in 2005? Determine the percentage of titles rented in June 2005.
BIRD Evidence: in June 2005 refers to month(rental_date) = 6 and year(rental_date) = 2005; percentage = divide(count(inventory_id where month(rental_date) = 6 and year(rental_date) = 2005), count(inventory_id)) * 100%
Gold DB: movie_3 | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: sakila_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT 
    COUNT(*) AS total_rentals,
    ROUND((COUNT(CASE WHEN strftime('%Y-%m', rental_date) = '2005-06' THEN 1 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*)), 2) AS june_percentage
FROM rental r
JOIN customer c ON r.customer_id = c.customer_id
JOIN inventory i ON r.inventory_id = i.inventory_id
JOIN film f ON i.film_id = f.film_id
WHERE c.first_name = 'Mary' 
AND c.last_name = 'Smith'
AND strftime('%Y', rental_date) = '2005';
Selected SQL: SELECT 
    (SELECT COUNT(*) 
     FROM rental r 
     JOIN customer c ON r.customer_id = c.customer_id 
     JOIN inventory i ON r.inventory_id = i.inventory_id 
     JOIN film f ON i.film_id = f.film_id 
     WHERE c.first_name = 'Mary' AND c.last_name = 'Smith' 
     AND strftime('%Y', r.rental_date) = '2005') AS total_rentals,
    (COUNT(*) * 100.0 / (SELECT COUNT(*) 
                         FROM rental r 
                         JOIN customer c ON r.customer_id = c.customer_id 
                         JOIN inventory i ON r.inventory_id = i.inventory_id 
                         JOIN film f ON i.film_id = f.film_id 
                         WHERE c.first_name = 'Mary' AND c.last_name = 'Smith' 
                         AND strftime('%Y', r.rental_date) = '2005')) AS june_percentage
FROM rental r 
JOIN customer c ON r.customer_id = c.customer_id 
JOIN inventory i ON r.inventory_id = i.inventory_id 
JOIN film f ON i.film_id = f.film_id 
WHERE c.first_name = 'Mary' AND c.last_name = 'Smith'

[Failure 824] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error
Query: Please give the ids of the oldest films that got the most ratings.
BIRD Evidence: Films and movies share the same meaning; oldest film refers to the movie with year = 1
Gold DB: movielens | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: movie_1 | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: WITH rating_counts AS (
    SELECT movieid, COUNT(*) AS num_ratings
    FROM u2base
    GROUP BY movieid
),
max_ratings AS (
    SELECT MAX(num_ratings) AS max_count
    FROM rating_counts
),
oldest_movies AS (
    SELECT m.movieid, m.year
    FROM movies m
    JOIN rating_counts rc ON m.movieid = rc.movieid
    JOIN max_ratings mr ON rc.num_ratings = mr.max_count
    ORDER BY m.year ASC
    LIMIT 1
)
SELECT movieid FROM oldest_movies;
Selected SQL: SELECT mID
FROM (
    SELECT m.mID, COUNT(*) AS rating_count
    FROM Movie m
    JOIN Rating r ON m.mID = r.mID
    WHERE m.year = (SELECT MIN(year) FROM Movie)
    GROUP BY m.mID
    ORDER BY rating_count DESC
    LIMIT 1
);

Gold DB: simpson_episodes | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: law_episode | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT e.title, v.stars, v.votes
FROM Episode e
JOIN Vote v ON e.episode_id = v.episode_id
WHERE v.stars = (SELECT MIN(stars) FROM Vote)
ORDER BY v.votes DESC
LIMIT 3;
Selected SQL: SELECT e.episode_id, e.title, v.stars, v.votes
FROM Episode e
JOIN Vote v ON e.episode_id = v.episode_id
WHERE v.stars = (SELECT MIN(stars) FROM Vote)
ORDER BY v.votes DESC
LIMIT 3;

[Failure 888] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error
Query: Among the patients whose creatinine level is abnormal, how many of them aren't 70 yet?
BIRD Evidence: creatinine level is abnormal refers to CRE >= 1.5; aren't 70 yet refers to SUBTRACT((YEAR(CURDATE()), YEAR(Birthday))) < 70; 
Gold DB: thrombosis_prediction | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: synthea | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT Patient.ID)
FROM Patient
JOIN Laboratory ON Patient.ID = Laboratory.ID
WHERE Laboratory.CRE NOT BETWEEN 60 AND 110
AND (strftime('%Y', 'now') - strftime('%Y', Patient.Birthday)) < 70;
Selected SQL: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT p.patient)
FROM patients p
JOIN observations o ON p.patient = o.patient
WHERE o.DESCRIPTION LIKE '%creatinine%' 
  AND o.VALUE NOT BETWEEN 0.6 AND 1.3
  AND (julianday('now') - julianday(p.birthdate)) / 365.25 < 70;

Gold SQL: SELECT st.Name, SUM(soh.TotalDue) AS TotalRevenue

JOIN SalesOrderHeader soh ON st.TerritoryID = soh.TerritoryID

[Failure 900] - CATEGORY: Populated Ambiguity / Judge Error

BIRD Evidence: profit = SUBTRACT(ListPrice, StandardCost);
Gold DB: works_cycles | Status: POPULATED
Selected DB: car_retails | Status: POPULATED
Gold SQL: SELECT p.Name, SUM(sod.LineTotal - (p.StandardCost * sod.OrderQty)) AS Profit

LIMIT 1;
